# OK <verified> (level 35)
A B C.: OK / A. B. C: okay | :1
A B C.: OK's / A. B. C: okay's | :1
A B C.: OKed / A. B. C: okayed | :1
A B C.: OKing / A. B. C: okaying | :1
A B C.: OKs / A. B. C: okays | :1
A B: OK | <abbr> Oklahoma
## OK is generally the preferred form, but it is very difficult to
## misspell one for the other and in some contexts okay is preferred,
## so I am marking these as equal variants.  Note that the Canadian
## Ox. has okay as the primary form.

## be a valid word, this spelling was not included.
